This LLD covers `/login`, `/signup`, `/chat`, `/chat/[conversationId]`, the WS streaming reducer, the user-scoped conversation list, logout, the typed WS client, and the \"N earlier messages omitted\" indicator. Phase B (`/console`) is out of scope.\n15\t\n16\tThis LLD assumes `packages/contracts` (authored by the backend/contracts LLD per HLD D2) exports the WS frame discriminated union, REST DTOs for auth + conversations, and the OTel attribute schema. Frontend-web consumes those types and does not redeclare them. If `packages/contracts` is not yet available when a frontend task begins, the frontend worker stubs the import surface against the HLD-defined frame names (`start`, `token`, `end`, `error`, `cancel-ack`, `canceled`, plus client→server `send` and `cancel`) and the backend/contracts LLD reconciles on landing.\n17\t\n18\t## Builder\n19\t**agent:** frontend-web-worker\n20\t**model:** opus\n21\t\n22\t## Reviewer (cross-model — REQUIRED different lineage)\n23\t**mechanism:** `oh-cross-model --model codex`\n24\t**framing:** see `~/.claude/skills/oh/prompts/builder-addendum.md`\n25\t\n26\t## Tester (cross-model — REQUIRED different lineage)\n27\t**mechanism:** `oh-cross-model --model codex`\n28\t**framing:** test-writer agent assembles the test plan; codex designs the actual tests via the wrapper\n29\t\n30\t## File Structure\n31\t\n32\tEach file has one clear responsibility. Auth and chat are colocated under Next.js App Router route groups; reusable chat pieces live under `apps/web/components/chat`; transport and data fetching live under `apps/web/lib`.\n33\t\n34\t### Routes / pages (Next.js App Router under `apps/web/app/`)\n35\t\n36\t- `apps/web/app/(auth)/layout.tsx` — minimal layout wrapper for the auth route group (no nav, centered card).\n37\t- `apps/web/app/(auth)/login/page.tsx` — client component hosting the login form, inline error states, post-success redirect to `/chat`.\n38\t- `apps/web/app/(auth)/signup/page.tsx` — client component hosting the signup form including duplicate-email inline error and post-success redirect to `/chat`.\n39\t- `apps/web/app/chat/layout.tsx` — auth-gated layout: server-side session check, renders sidebar (`ConversationList`) plus child content; redirects unauthenticated requests to `/login`.\n40\t- `apps/web/app/chat/page.tsx` — default new-conversation shell: empty chat surface ready to accept the first user message; on first send, navigates to `/chat/[conversationId]` once the server mints the conversation id.\n41\t- `apps/web/app/chat/[conversationId]/page.tsx` — resume view: server-side fetch of message history for that conversation (filtered by user), passes initial messages to the `MessageStream` client component.\n42\t\n43\t### Chat components (`apps/web/components/chat/`)\n44\t\n45\t- `apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx` — client component: holds the per-conversation message log in state via a discriminated-frame reducer; renders messages, the streaming assistant bubble, the cancel button, the retry button on failed turns, the \"interrupted\" marker after refresh-during-stream, the active-provider label per turn, and the \"N earlier messages omitted from context\" indicator. Disables the composer while streaming.\n46\t- `apps/web/components/chat/MessageComposer.tsx` — client component: input + send button; controlled disabled state driven from `MessageStream` via prop; emits `onSend(text)` upward.\n47\t- `apps/web/components/chat/MessageList.tsx` — pure render component for the message log array; no state of its own; renders each message based on `role` and `status`.\n48\t- `apps/web/components/chat/ConversationList.tsx` — client component: server-fetched user-scoped list, renders empty state (\"No conversations yet — start a new chat\") when empty, highlights the active conversation, link-navigates to `/chat/[id]`.\n49\t- `apps/web/components/chat/LogoutButton.tsx` — client component: one-click POST to `/api/auth/logout`, then router push to `/login`.\n50\t- `apps/web/components/chat/OmittedIndicator.tsx` — pure render component: shows \"N earlier messages omitted from context\" when N > 0, hidden otherwise.\n51\t\n52\t### Reducer + transport (`apps/web/lib/`)\n53\t\n54\t- `apps/web/lib/message-stream-reducer.ts` — pure reducer: takes current per-conversation log state plus an inbound frame (or local action like `cancel-requested`, `retry-clicked`, `composer-submitted`), returns the next log state. Owns the cancel-race rule (late tokens arriving after a canceled terminal are dropped). Exported separately from `MessageStream.tsx` so it's unit-testable without React.\n55\t- `apps/web/lib/ws-client.ts` — typed WS client class: takes the server WS URL, opens the socket with cookies, exposes `send(frame)`, an async iterator or callback-based `onFrame(handler)` for inbound frames, validates every inbound frame against the `packages/contracts` zod schema, surfaces a typed `onClose` and `onError`, and supports `close()` for unmount cleanup.\n56\t- `apps/web/lib/auth-fetch.ts` — thin wrapper over `fetch` that forwards the session cookie, throws a typed `AuthError` on 401 so callers can redirect to `/login`, and returns parsed JSON.\n57\t- `apps/web/lib/conversations-api.ts` — REST helpers: `listConversations()`, `getConversation(id)`, `getMessages(conversationId)` — each calls `auth-fetch` and returns typed DTOs from `packages/contracts`.\n58\t- `apps/web/lib/server-session.ts` — server-only helper: reads the session cookie from `next/headers`, calls the API's `/auth/session` (or equivalent) to resolve to a user, returns `null` on missing/invalid. Used by `app/chat/layout.tsx`.\n59\t\n60\t### Test files (`apps/web/__tests__/` mirrors source path)\n61\t\n62\t- `apps/web/__tests__/lib/message-stream-reducer.test.ts` — unit tests for the reducer across every frame transition.\n63\t- `apps/web/__tests__/lib/ws-client.test.ts` — unit tests using a mocked WebSocket constructor.\n64\t- `apps/web/__tests__/components/MessageStream.test.tsx` — React Testing Library tests for the user-facing behavior (cancel button visible during stream, retry visible on fail, composer disabled during stream).\n65\t- `apps/web/__tests__/components/ConversationList.test.tsx` — RTL tests for empty state and selected state.\n66\t- `apps/web/__tests__/components/OmittedIndicator.test.tsx` — RTL tests for visibility threshold.\n67\t- `apps/web/__tests__/components/LogoutButton.test.tsx` — RTL test for click → fetch invoked with correct path.\n68\t\n69\t### Config / scaffolding (`apps/web/`)\n70\t\n71\t- `apps/web/package.json` — Next.js 14+ app, scripts for `dev`, `build`, `start`, `type-check`, `lint`, `test`.\n72\t- `apps/web/tsconfig.json` — strict TS, path alias to `packages/contracts`.\n73\t- `apps/web/next.config.mjs` — minimal config; rewrites for `/api/*` to `apps/api`.\n74\t- `apps/web/vitest.config.ts` — Vitest + jsdom + RTL setup.\n75\t- `apps/web/vitest.setup.ts` — global RTL cleanup, jest-dom matchers.\n76\t- `apps/web/app/layout.tsx` — root layout (html/body) with global CSS.\n77\t- `apps/web/app/globals.css` — Tailwind base + minimal global styles.\n78\t- `apps/web/tailwind.config.ts` + `apps/web/postcss.config.mjs` — Tailwind setup (matches the rest of the monorepo convention).\n79\t\n80\t---\n81\t\n82\t## Tasks\n83\t\n84\t> Verify commands assume working directory `apps/web` unless absolute, and that pnpm is the package manager (matches HLD's `Turborepo + pnpm` lock from the brief).\n85\t\n86\t### Task 1: [non-TDD — Next.js app scaffolding] Drives the chat surface. Decoupled from React so it can be unit-tested\n3\t// without rendering anything.\n4\t//\n5\t// LLD references:\n6\t//   Task 3-16   per-frame and per-action transitions\n7\t//   Task 42     init carries `omittedCount`\n8\t//   Task 57     terminal error before any `start` (e.g. no_providers_available)\n9\t//\n10\t// Key invariants (HLD Regression Risk Surface):\n11\t//   - A message_id that has reached a terminal state (complete/canceled/failed)\n12\t//     is immutable. Late `token` frames for it are dropped, not appended.\n13\t//   - `composerDisabled` flips to `true` on `composer-submitted` and back to\n14\t//     `false` only on a terminal frame (`end` with any status, or `error`).\n15\t//   - The reducer is pure: same (state, action) -> same nextState reference\n16\t//     when no change applies (used by tests to assert \"second submit is a\n17\t//     no-op\").\n18\t//\n19\t// All identifiers stay in the contracts vocabulary (`messageId` camelCase per\n20\t// `@argus/contracts/ws`).\n21\t\n22\timport type {\n23\t  WsEndFrame,\n24\t  WsErrorFrame,\n25\t  WsFrameOutbound,\n26\t  WsStartFrame,\n27\t  WsTokenFrame,\n28\t} from '@argus/contracts';\n29\t\n30\texport type MessageRole = 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system';\n31\t\n32\texport type MessageStatus = 'streaming' | 'complete' | 'failed' | 'canceled';\n33\t\n34\t/**\n35\t * Message — the per-row shape rendered in the message list. Wide enough to\n36\t * cover both user-authored messages (no provider/model) and assistant turns\n37\t * (carry provider/model + optional errorCode on failure).\n38\t */\n39\texport type Message = {\n40\t  id: string;\n41\t  role: MessageRole;\n42\t  content: string;\n43\t  status: MessageStatus;\n44\t  provider?: string;\n45\t  model?: string;\n46\t  /** Set true on failed messages that can be retried. */\n47\t  canRetry?: boolean;\n48\t  /** WS error_code (or restored from history) — drives \"interrupted\" marker. */\n49\t  errorCode?: string;\n50\t  /** Highest `seq` applied for this streaming message (drops out-of-order). */\n51\t  lastAppliedSeq?: number;\n52\t};\n53\t\n54\t/**\n55\t * Streaming view of the assistant bubble currently being built up. Same shape\n56\t * as `Message` but kept separate from `messages` so renderers can show the\n57\t * caret animation under it without scanning the whole list.\n58\t */\n59\texport type StreamingMessage = Message;\n60\t\n61\texport type TerminalError = {\n62\t  errorCode: string;\n63\t  message?: string;\n64\t};\n65\t\n66\texport type State = {\n67\t  messages: Message[];\n68\t  streaming: StreamingMessage | null;\n69\t  /** Locks the composer while an assistant turn is in flight. */\n70\t  composerDisabled: boolean;\n71\t  /** Number of older messages dropped by context cap (HLD D6 indicator). */\n72\t  omittedCount: number;\n73\t  /** Set on terminal errors that prevent a turn from starting (e.g. no providers). */\n74\t  terminalError: TerminalError | null;\n75\t};\n76\t\n77\texport const initialState: State = {\n78\t  messages: [],\n79\t  streaming: null,\n80\t  composerDisabled: false,\n81\t  omittedCount: 0,\n82\t  terminalError: null,\n83\t};\n84\t\n85\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n86\t// Action union — server frames + local user actions both flow through here.\n87\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n88\t\n89\texport type Action =\n90\t  | {\n91\t      type: 'init';\n92\t      messages: Message[];\n93\t      omittedCount?: number;\n94\t    }\n95\t  | {\n96\t      type: 'frame';\n97\t      frame: WsFrameOutbound;\n98\t    }\n99\t  | {\n100\t      type: 'composer-submitted';\n101\t      /** Locally-generated optimistic id for the user row. */\n102\t      userMessageId: string;\n103\t      text: string;\n104\t    };\n105\t\n106\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n107\t// Reducer.\n108\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n109\t\n110\texport function reducer(state: State, action: Action): State {\n111\t  switch (action.type) {\n112\t    case 'init':\n113\t      return {\n114\t        ...initialState,\n115\t        messages: action.messages,\n116\t        omittedCount: action.omittedCount ?? 0,\n117\t      };\n118\t\n119\t    case 'composer-submitted': {\n120\t      // Single-in-flight lock — second submit while streaming is a no-op.\n121\t      // Return the SAME reference so callers can assert idempotency.\n122\t      if (state.composerDisabled) {\n123\t        return state;\n124\t      }\n125\t      const userRow: Message = {\n126\t        id: action.userMessageId,\n127\t        role: 'user',\n128\t        content: action.text,\n129\t        status: 'complete',\n130\t      };\n131\t      return {\n132\t        ...state,\n133\t        messages: [...state.messages, userRow],\n134\t        composerDisabled: true,\n135\t        // A fresh submit clears any prior terminalError banner.\n136\t        terminalError: null,\n137\t      };\n138\t    }\n139\t\n140\t    case 'frame':\n141\t      return applyFrame(state, action.frame);\n142\t  }\n143\t}\n144\t\n145\tfunction applyFrame(state: State, frame: WsFrameOutbound): State {\n146\t  switch (frame.type) {\n147\t    case 'start':\n148\t      return applyStart(state, frame);\n149\t    case 'token':\n150\t      return applyToken(state, frame);\n151\t    case 'end':\n152\t      return applyEnd(state, frame);\n153\t    case 'error':\n154\t      return applyError(state, frame);\n155\t    case 'cancel-ack':\n156\t      // The user-visible Cancel button can be dimmed via local state in the\n157\t      // component if desired; the reducer treats cancel-ack as informational.\n158\t      // The actual terminal transition arrives via the subsequent `end`.\n159\t      return state;\n160\t  }\n161\t}\n162\t\n163\tfunction applyStart(state: State, frame: WsStartFrame): State {\n164\t  // If a message_id has already terminated, ignore (defense against the\n165\t  // server replaying a frame after a terminal — should never happen, but the\n166\t  // invariant is cheap to enforce).\n167\t  if (isTerminal(state, frame.messageId)) {\n168\t    return state;\n169\t  }\n170\t  const streaming: StreamingMessage = {\n171\t    id: frame.messageId,\n172\t    role: 'assistant',\n173\t    content: '',\n174\t    status: 'streaming',\n175\t    provider: frame.provider,\n176\t    model: frame.model,\n177\t    lastAppliedSeq: 0,\n178\t  };\n179\t  return {\n180\t    ...state,\n181\t    streaming,\n182\t    composerDisabled: true,\n183\t  };\n184\t}\n185\t\n186\tfunction applyToken(state: State, frame: WsTokenFrame): State {\n187\t  // Drop if this message has terminated (HLD Regression Risk: cancel race).\n188\t  if (isTerminal(state, frame.messageId)) {\n189\t    return state;\n190\t  }\n191\t  const current = state.streaming;\n192\t  // Token for an unknown bubble (no prior start) — drop. The server should\n193\t  // never do this, but the reducer stays defensive.\n194\t  if (!current || current.id !== frame.messageId) {\n195\t    return state;\n196\t  }\n197\t  const lastSeq = current.lastAppliedSeq ?? 0;\n198\t  // Out-of-order or replayed delivery — drop.\n199\t  if (frame.seq <= lastSeq) {\n200\t    return state;\n201\t  }\n202\t  const nextStreaming: StreamingMessage = {\n203\t    ...current,\n204\t    content: current.content + frame.content,\n205\t    lastAppliedSeq: frame.seq,\n206\t  };\n207\t  return { ...state, streaming: nextStreaming };\n208\t}\n209\t\n210\tfunction applyEnd(state: State, frame: WsEndFrame): State {\n211\t  if (isTerminal(state, frame.messageId)) {\n212\t    return state;\n213\t  }\n214\t  const current = state.streaming;\n215\t  // End without a streaming bubble — nothing to promote. Could happen on a\n216\t  // server bug or a reconnect race; treat as a no-op so the reducer stays\n217\t  // monotonic.\n218\t  if (!current || current.id !== frame.messageId) {\n219\t    return state;\n220\t  }\n221\t  const promoted: Message = {\n222\t    ...current,\n223\t    status: frame.status,\n224\t    // canRetry surfaces on failed messages so the UI can show Retry; canceled\n225\t    // and complete messages don't expose retry.\n226\t    canRetry: frame.status === 'failed',\n227\t    lastAppliedSeq: undefined,\n228\t  };\n229\t  return {\n230\t    ...state,\n231\t    streaming: null,\n232\t    messages: [...state.messages, promoted],\n233\t    composerDisabled: false,\n234\t  };\n235\t}\n236\t\n237\tfunction applyError(state: State, frame: WsErrorFrame): State {\n238\t  // Two distinct shapes:\n239\t  //   1. error with an active streaming bubble whose id matches → promote\n240\t  //      bubble to status=failed, preserve partial content, set canRetry.\n241\t  //   2. error without an active bubble → record a terminalError banner.\n242\t  //      LLD Task 57 specifies this only happens when the gateway can't pick\n243\t  //      a provider (no_providers_available); other top-level codes still\n244\t  //      get surfaced via terminalError so the UI can render something\n245\t  //      instead of going silent.\n246\t  const current = state.streaming;\n247\t  if (current && frame.messageId && current.id === frame.messageId) {\n248\t    if (isTerminal(state, frame.messageId)) {\n249\t      return state;\n250\t    }\n251\t    const promoted: Message = {\n252\t      ...current,\n253\t      status: 'failed',\n254\t      canRetry: true,\n255\t      errorCode: frame.errorCode,\n256\t      lastAppliedSeq: undefined,\n257\t    };\n258\t    return {\n259\t      ...state,\n260\t      streaming: null,\n261\t      messages: [...state.messages, promoted],\n262\t      composerDisabled: false,\n263\t    };\n264\t  }\n265\t  // No active bubble — terminal error banner.\n266\t  return {\n267\t    ...state,\n268\t    terminalError: {\n269\t      errorCode: frame.errorCode,\n270\t      ...(frame.message !== undefined ? { message: frame.message } : {}),\n271\t    },\n272\t    composerDisabled: false,\n273\t  };\n274\t}\n275\t\n276\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n277\t// Helpers.\n278\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n279\t\n280\tfunction isTerminal(state: State, messageId: string): boolean {\n281\t  // A message_id is terminal if it appears in `messages` with any of the\n282\t  // terminal statuses. in\n11\t// production the default factory creates a `WsClient` pointed at\n12\t// `NEXT_PUBLIC_WS_URL` (resolved in `ws-client.ts`).\n13\t'use client';\n14\t\n15\timport {\n16\t  useCallback,\n17\t  useEffect,\n18\t  useMemo,\n19\t  useReducer,\n20\t  useRef,\n21\t  useState,\n22\t} from 'react';\n23\timport { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';\n24\t\n25\timport {\n26\t  initialState,\n27\t  reducer,\n28\t  type Message,\n29\t} from '@/lib/message-stream-reducer';\n30\timport {\n31\t  WsClient,\n32\t  type ErrorHandler,\n33\t  type FrameHandler,\n34\t  type CloseHandler,\n35\t} from '@/lib/ws-client';\n36\timport { MessageComposer } from './MessageComposer';\n37\timport { MessageList } from './MessageList';\n38\timport { OmittedIndicator } from './OmittedIndicator';\n39\timport { Mark } from '@/components/brand/Mark';\n40\timport type { WsFrameInbound } from '@argus/contracts';\n41\t\n42\t/**\n43\t * Subset of WsClient that MessageStream actually consumes — exposed for the\n44\t * test harness so a stub doesn't have to implement the entire class\n45\t * (including constructor side effects).\n46\t */\n47\texport type WsClientLike = {\n48\t  onFrame: (handler: FrameHandler) => void;\n49\t  onError: (handler: ErrorHandler) => void;\n50\t  onClose: (handler: CloseHandler) => void;\n51\t  send: (frame: WsFrameInbound) => void;\n52\t  close: () => void;\n53\t};\n54\t\n55\ttype MessageStreamProps = {\n56\t  conversationId: string | null;\n57\t  initialMessages: Message[];\n58\t  omittedCount?: number;\n59\t  /**\n60\t   * Optional WsClient. Stored in a ref because `router.replace` is the\n80\t  // side effect; we don't render off this value.\n81\t  const liveConvIdRef = useRef<string | null>(conversationId);\n82\t  useEffect(() => {\n83\t    liveConvIdRef.current = conversationId;\n84\t  }, [conversationId]);\n85\t\n86\t  // Hydrate the reducer once with the initial server-fetched history.\n87\t  useEffect(() => {\n88\t    dispatch({ type: 'init', messages: initialMessages, omittedCount });\n89\t    // We intentionally only run on mount — re-running on prop change would\n90\t    // wipe live in-flight state. If the consumer navigates to a different\n91\t    // conversation, the route change unmounts and remounts this component.\n92\t    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n93\t  }, []);\n94\t\n95\t  // Build / take the WsClient. In production we lazily instantiate one\n96\t  // tied to the component lifetime; in tests an injected stub takes over.\n97\t  const clientRef = useRef<WsClientLike | null>(null);\n98\t  if (clientRef.current === null) {\n99\t    clientRef.current = wsClient ?? new WsClient();\n100\t  }\n101\t  const client = clientRef.current;\n102\t\n103\t  useEffect(() => {\n104\t    const onFrame: FrameHandler = (frame) => {\n105\t      // On the first `start` frame for a brand-new conversation, learn the\n106\t      // freshly-minted conversation id and swap the URL so reload works.\n107\t      if (\n108\t        frame.type === 'start' &&\n109\t        liveConvIdRef.current === null &&\n110\t        frame.conversationId\n111\t      ) {\n112\t        liveConvIdRef.current = frame.conversationId;\n113\t        router.replace(`/chat/${frame.conversationId}`);\n114\t      }\n115\t      dispatch({ type: 'frame', frame });\n116\t    };\n117\t    const onError: ErrorHandler = (err) => {\n118\t      // Surface as a soft banner — the reducer's terminalError is reserved\n119\t      // for server-emitted error frames.\n120\t      setWsError(`Connection issue (${err.reason}). Please retry.`);\n121\t    };\n122\t    const onClose: CloseHandler = (_code) => {\n123\t      setWsReady(false);\n124\t    };\n125\t    client.onFrame(onFrame);\n126\t    client.onError(onError);\n127\t    client.onClose(onClose);\n128\t    setWsReady(true);\n129\t    return () => {\n130\t      client.close();\n131\t    };\n132\t    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n133\t  }, []);\n134\t\n135\t  // Last user message text — used for Retry resends (LLD Task 38).\n136\t  const lastUserText = useMemo(() => {\n137\t    for (let i = state.messages.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n138\t      const m = state.messages[i];\n139\t      if (m && m.role === 'user') {\n140\t        return m.content;\n141\t      }\n142\t    }\n143\t    return null;\n144\t  }, [state.messages]);\n145\t\n146\t  // Send handler.\n147\t  const handleSend = useCallback(\n148\t    (text: string) => {\n149\t      const userMessageId = uuidv4Safe();\n150\t      dispatch({ type: 'composer-submitted', userMessageId, text });\n151\t      // Defensive: if WS not ready, surface and bail. Reducer will have\n152\t      // optimistically appended the user message; if the user retries we'll\n153\t      // pick it up.\n154\t      try {\n155\t        client.send({\n156\t          type: 'send',\n157\t          conversationId: liveConvIdRef.current,\n158\t          content: text,\n159\t        });\n160\t      } catch (err) {\n161\t        setWsError(`Could not send: ${(err as Error).message}`);\n162\t      }\n163\t    },\n164\t    [client],\n165\t  );\n166\t\n167\t  // Retry handler — re-send the last user text. The reducer's\n168\t  // `composer-submitted` lock is already cleared (terminal error released\n169\t  // it), so the dispatch goes through.\n170\t  const handleRetry = useCallback(\n171\t    (_failedMessageId: string) => {\n172\t      if (!lastUserText) return;\n173\t      const userMessageId = uuidv4Safe();\n174\t      dispatch({ type: 'composer-submitted', userMessageId, text: lastUserText });\n175\t      try {\n176\t        client.send({\n177\t          type: 'send',\n178\t          conversationId: liveConvIdRef.current,\n179\t          content: lastUserText,\n180\t        });\n181\t      } catch (err) {\n182\t        setWsError(`Could not send: ${(err as Error).message}`);\n183\t      }\n184\t    },\n185\t    [client, lastUserText],\n186\t  );\n187\t\n188\t  // Cancel handler.\n189\t  const handleCancel = useCallback(() => {\n190\t    const active = state.streaming;\n191\t    if (!active) return;\n192\t    try {\n193\t      client.send({ type: 'cancel', messageId: active.id });\n194\t    } catch (err) {\n195\t      setWsError(`Could not cancel: ${(err as Error).message}`);\n196\t    }\n197\t  }, [client, state.streaming]);\n198\t\n199\t  const streaming = state.streaming;\n200\t\n201\t  return (\n202\t    <section\n203\t      data-testid=\"message-stream\"\n204\t      data-ws-ready={wsReady ? 'true' : 'false'}\n205\t      className=\"flex h-full flex-col\"\n206\t    >\n207\t      <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto\">\n208\t        {state.omittedCount > 0 ? (\n209\t          <div className=\"flex justify-center pt-4\">\n210\t            <OmittedIndicator count={state.omittedCount} />\n211\t          </div>\n212\t        ) : null}\n213\t\n214\t        {state.terminalError ? <TerminalErrorBanner code={state.terminalError.errorCode} /> : null}\n215\t\n216\t        <MessageList messages={state.messages} onRetry={handleRetry} />\n217\t\n218\t        {streaming ? We don't take a\n312\t * dependency on the `uuid` npm package for one call site.\n313\t */\n314\tfunction uuidv4Safe(): string {\n315\t  const cryptoObj = typeof globalThis !== 'undefined' ? globalThis.crypto : undefined;\n316\t  if (cryptoObj && typeof cryptoObj.randomUUID === 'function') {\n317\t    return cryptoObj.randomUUID();\n318\t  }\n319\t  // Fallback — not cryptographically strong but only used as a local id.\n320\t  return 'u-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);\n321\t}\n322\t\n323\t"}]},"uuid":"505e4400-7d48-4199-91b1-c03550098fd6","timestamp":"2026-05-23T19:44:28.085Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"d18a6355-f2b3-4d2b-83b7-8ed1512d3463","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"/Users/lego/Desktop/personal-projects/argus/.worktrees/phase-a-build","sessionId":"11d45e97-2fff-4114-aafb-b68d865b0473","version":"2.1.150","gitBranch":"HEAD"}

Two directions:\n4\t//\n5\t//   inbound  (client → server):\n6\t//     - send      kick off a turn against an existing conversation\n7\t//     - cancel    request server stop streaming an in-flight message\n8\t//\n9\t//   outbound (server → client):\n10\t//     - start         server has accepted the turn, message_id minted, provider chosen\n11\t//     - token         next chunk of assistant content\n12\t//     - end           terminal frame; carries final status (complete | canceled | failed)\n13\t//     - error         provider/server-side error (always followed by an `end`)\n14\t//     - cancel-ack    acknowledges receipt of a cancel request\n15\t//\n16\t// All outbound frames carry `seq` — strictly monotonic per message_id starting\n17\t// at 0 (start) → 1..N (token) → terminal end/cancel-ack/error.\n18\timport { z } from 'zod';\n19\t\n20\t// Path the @WebSocketGateway is mounted on. Web client and any wscat smoke\n21\t// test must dial this exact path.\n22\texport const WS_PATH = '/ws/chat';\n23\t\n24\t// Provider + model values are free-text at the wire boundary — the gateway\n25\t// does not constrain which providers the SDK supports.\n26\t\n27\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n28\t// Inbound (client → server)\n29\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n30\t\n31\texport const WsSendFrameSchema = z.object({\n32\t  type: z.literal('send'),\n33\t  // Null for the FIRST turn of a brand-new conversation — the gateway mints\n34\t  // both the conversation row and `message_id`, then surfaces the freshly\n35\t  // minted conversation id on the next `start` frame so the web client can\n36\t  // `router.replace(/chat/<id>)` (frontend-web LLD Tasks 52 + 54). Once a\n37\t  // conversation exists, every subsequent send carries its UUID.\n38\t  conversationId: z.string().uuid().nullable(),\n39\t  // The user-authored content for this turn. The server mints `message_id`\n40\t  // — client never assigns one (HLD D1 — gateway is sole minter).\n41\t  content: z.string().min(1).max(64_000),\n42\t});\n43\texport type WsSendFrame = z.infer<typeof WsSendFrameSchema>;\n44\t\n45\texport const WsCancelFrameSchema = z.object({\n46\t  type: z.literal('cancel'),\n47\t  // The assistant `message_id` previously delivered in a `start` frame.\n48\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n49\t});\n50\texport type WsCancelFrame = z.infer<typeof WsCancelFrameSchema>;\n51\t\n52\texport const WsFrameInboundSchema = z.discriminatedUnion('type', [\n53\t  WsSendFrameSchema,\n54\t  WsCancelFrameSchema,\n55\t]);\n56\texport type WsFrameInbound = z.infer<typeof WsFrameInboundSchema>;\n57\t\n58\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n59\t// Outbound (server → client)\n60\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n61\t\n62\texport const WsStartFrameSchema = z.object({\n63\t  type: z.literal('start'),\n64\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n65\t  conversationId: z.string().uuid(),\n66\t  provider: z.string(),\n67\t  model: z.string(),\n68\t  // Always 0 for start frames.\n69\t  seq: z.literal(0),\n70\t});\n71\texport type WsStartFrame = z.infer<typeof WsStartFrameSchema>;\n72\t\n73\texport const WsTokenFrameSchema = z.object({\n74\t  type: z.literal('token'),\n75\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n76\t  // Monotonic, strictly increasing from 1.\n77\t  seq: z.number().int().min(1),\n78\t  content: z.string(),\n79\t});\n80\texport type WsTokenFrame = z.infer<typeof WsTokenFrameSchema>;\n81\t\n82\texport const WsEndStatusSchema = z.enum(['complete', 'canceled', 'failed']);\n83\texport type WsEndStatus = z.infer<typeof WsEndStatusSchema>;\n84\t\n85\texport const WsEndFrameSchema = z.object({\n86\t  type: z.literal('end'),\n87\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n88\t  // Terminal seq — greater than every token seq emitted for this message.\n89\t  seq: z.number().int().min(1),\n90\t  status: WsEndStatusSchema,\n91\t});\n92\texport type WsEndFrame = z.infer<typeof WsEndFrameSchema>;\n93\t\n94\texport const WsErrorFrameSchema = z.object({\n95\t  type: z.literal('error'),\n96\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n97\t  errorCode: z.string(),\n98\t  message: z.string().optional(),\n99\t});\n100\texport type WsErrorFrame = z.infer<typeof WsErrorFrameSchema>;\n101\t\n102\texport const WsCancelAckFrameSchema = z.object({\n103\t  type: z.literal('cancel-ack'),\n104\t  messageId: z.string().uuid(),\n105\t});\n106\texport type WsCancelAckFrame = z.infer<typeof WsErrorFrameSchema,\n113\t  WsCancelAckFrameSchema,\n114\t]);\n115\texport type WsFrameOutbound = z.infer<typeof WsFrameOutboundSchema>;\n116\t\n117\t// Union of every frame type — useful for tests {"parentUuid":"0f3f65c5-b487-4a02-bf81-72732de8ad4f","isSidechain":true,"agentId":"aaecd9c60b4bd13d1","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-7","id":"msg_015sgo6BQRc35LiAbhhYdYeC","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"I now have sufficient context to deliver the review.\n\n---\n\n## 1. LLD adherence\n\n- **Task 25 acceptance gap (cosmetic):** LLD says `ws://localhost:4000/chat`; `ws-client` defaults to `ws://localhost:4000/ws/chat`. This matches the contract `WS_PATH='/ws/chat'`, so the LLD was wrong, not the code — fine, but note the deviation.\n- **Vitest → Jest** swap documented in `jest.config.js` header; acceptable, mirrors the rest of the monorepo.\n- **`vitest.setup.ts` / `tsconfig.test.json`** not delivered — replaced by `jest.config.js` + `jest.setup.ts`. Functionally equivalent.\n- **`apps/web/components/brand/Mark.tsx` & `Wordmark.tsx`** added (not in LLD file list) — fine, design-fidelity supports them.\n- **Task 47** acceptance asks for \"5xx render a generic\" — login page bunches 5xx + network into the same branch. OK.\n- **No `ConversationListActive` in the LLD** — it was added because `usePathname` is client-only. Reasonable per Open Question 5, documented.\n- **No smoke test artifact (Task 58)** — manual-only by design.\n\n## 2. Correctness bugs\n\n1. **`apps/web/lib/auth-fetch.ts:49-55` + server-side callers — broken path on `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` configured deployments.** The Next rewrite `/api/:path*` → `${apiOrigin}/:path*` strips the `/api` prefix. Browser fetches to `/api/auth/login` arrive at the api as `/auth/login` (api controllers are `@Controller('auth')` with no global prefix — confirmed). But `server-session.ts:40` and `conversations-api.ts:20,32` call `authFetch('/api/...')` directly server-side, where `apiBaseUrl()` returns `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` and bypasses rewrites entirely → final URL `http://api:4000/api/auth/session`, which the api returns 404 on. Same problem when env is unset: `apiBaseUrl()` returns `''`, fetch gets a relative URL `/api/auth/session`, and Node's `fetch` throws \"Invalid URL\" on the server (Next 15 server fetch requires an absolute URL). Either give server-side calls a separate `API_INTERNAL_URL` env (different from the browser rewrite source), or have `auth-fetch` strip `/api` when adding `baseUrl`, or have controllers use `setGlobalPrefix('api')`. As shipped, no `/chat` page can ever load — the layout will throw, hit `error.tsx`, and `getSessionUser` will return null on every render → infinite redirect to `/login`.\n\n2. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:96-100` — WsClient instantiated in module render path on the server.** `clientRef.current = wsClient ?? new WsClient()` runs during render. The `MessageStream` is rendered from a Server Component (`app/chat/page.tsx` and `app/chat/[conversationId]/page.tsx`) at the boundary; with the `'use client'` directive the body runs client-side at hydration time, so this is OK in production. BUT during SSR, `useRef` runs once on the server too, and then the `if (clientRef.current === null)` evaluation re-runs on the client mount — `useRef` initial value being `null` and then mutated in the render body is a well-known React anti-pattern that misbehaves under `StrictMode` double-invoke and breaks SSR-safety: server-side, `new WebSocket(...)` throws (no `WebSocket` global in Node). Move construction into `useEffect` (`useState(() => null)` + lazy init, or `useRef` with init in `useEffect`).\n\n3. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:128-130` — unmount closes a stub client, breaking React StrictMode mount/unmount/mount cycle.** In dev with StrictMode (enabled per `next.config.mjs`), the effect runs twice: mount → cleanup (`client.close()`) → mount. The second mount keeps the same `clientRef.current` (closed); subsequent `client.send` throws \"not connected (closed)\" and `onFrame` never fires. The same effect also calls `setWsReady(true)` after `client.onFrame(...)` — fine for tests that pass a stub, but in prod with the real socket, `setWsReady(true)` fires before `onopen`, so the gating is misleading.\n\n4. **`apps/web/lib/message-stream-reducer.ts:163-184` — `applyStart` does not reset `lastAppliedSeq` on a retry of the same message_id.** If the server (against spec) reuses a `messageId` after a `failed` end, the `isTerminal` guard drops the second `start`. That's correct, but the test in `__tests__/lib/message-stream-reducer.test.ts:177-198` and the Retry flow in `MessageStream.tsx:170-186` generate a NEW `userMessageId` for retry — fine — but the assistant `messageId` will be a different server-minted id, so the guard doesn't bite. Net: no actual bug; flagged for the reader.\n\n5. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:147-165` — `handleSend` is dispatched BEFORE `client.send` succeeds.** If `client.send` throws (CONNECTING readyState), the reducer has already appended the user message and set `composerDisabled=true`, but no `end`/`error` frame will ever arrive to release the lock. The composer is permanently disabled until unmount. Either send first then dispatch, or dispatch a synthetic `error` frame in the catch to release the lock.\n\n6. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:170-186` — Retry duplicates the user message in the transcript.** Per builder concern #7 and LLD Task 38: \"Retry … dispatch a `composer-submitted` action for the most recent user message's text\". The retry handler dispatches `composer-submitted` which appends a NEW user-row to `messages` (reducer line 132). After retry, the transcript shows: `user(\"hello\")`, `assistant(failed)`, `user(\"hello\")` again. The LLD/PRD intent is that Retry retries the same turn without re-rendering the user message. Fix: introduce a new `retry-clicked` action that only flips `composerDisabled` and calls `wsClient.send`, without appending a row.\n\n7. **`apps/web/lib/message-stream-reducer.ts:247-264` — `applyError` matches `frame.messageId` against the streaming bubble but the schema requires `messageId` is always present (uuid, never null).** The `current && frame.messageId && current.id === frame.messageId` check has dead branches (`frame.messageId` is always truthy). The reducer logic is fine, but the comment in `__tests__/lib/message-stream-reducer.test.ts:65` says \"for the 'no active stream' case we still pass a synthetic messageId\" — and indeed the test for `no_providers_available` (line 252) uses MSG_ID. The terminal-error path is only chosen because `state.streaming === null`. If a stream is active and `no_providers_available` arrives carrying the streaming bubble's messageId, it'll be treated as a per-message failure with `canRetry=true` and no terminal banner. That contradicts Task 56's \"happens before provider selection succeeds\" semantics — minor in practice (server won't emit no_providers_available mid-stream) but worth a guard: branch on `errorCode === 'no_providers_available'` first.\n\n8. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:208` — `state.omittedCount` is set only via `init`.** Mount-time `useEffect` dispatches `init` with `omittedCount` (line 88). But the `useEffect` runs AFTER the first paint, so the first render shows `omittedCount: 0` from `initialState`. With omitted=5, you get a one-frame flash where the indicator is missing. Either compute initial state via `useReducer(reducer, undefined, () => ({...initialState, messages: initialMessages, omittedCount}))` or render directly from props until init runs.\n\n9. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:113` — `router.replace(/chat/${frame.conversationId})` runs inside the reducer dispatch path, which is a side-effect.** That's a `useReducer` side-effect-in-handler — technically OK because `onFrame` is the source, not the reducer, but if React StrictMode double-invokes the effect, the same `start` frame would call `router.replace` twice. Mitigated by the `liveConvIdRef.current === null` guard, which flips after the first call. OK.\n\n10. **`apps/web/components/chat/ConversationListActive.tsx:22` — pathname regex `^\\/chat\\/([0-9a-f-]{36})` only matches lowercase-hex UUIDs.** The contracts use `z.string().uuid()` which accepts mixed case. Use `/i` flag (it's there at the end of the regex — `i` IS present, so OK). Disregard.\n\n11. **`apps/web/components/chat/LogoutButton.tsx:24` — after a 401 from `/api/auth/logout` (e.g. session already expired), the user is shown a \"Could not log out\" error and stays on /chat.** That's user-hostile when the user actually wants to leave. Treat 401 as \"already logged out\" — push to `/login` anyway.\n\n12. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:218-253` — streaming bubble's `Cancel` button uses `<button>` inside a `<div>` adjacent to the message text spans.** ARIA-wise fine; visually the prototype puts cancel as a separate control bar, not inline with the meta dots. Minor design deviation; design-review owns the call.\n\n13. **`apps/web/components/chat/MessageStream.tsx:282-289` — `TerminalErrorBanner` README link uses `href=\"/README.md#providers\"`.** Next won't serve `README.md` from the repo root; in production the link 404s. Use an external GitHub URL or a real in-app docs page.\n\n14. **`apps/web/lib/ws-client.ts:74-80` — `onerror` fires before any handler is registered.** Constructor wires `socket.onerror` immediately, but the consumer's `onError` handler is set later via `client.onError(h)`. Any error event between `new WebSocket(...)` and the consumer's `useEffect` setup is silently dropped (`this.errorHandler?.(...)` short-circuits when null). Not exploitable in practice since the network is async, but buffer the first error or expose `onOpen`.\n\n## 3. Next 15 / React 19 specific issues\n\n- `cookies()` — correctly awaited in `server-session.ts:28` and `server-session.ts:63`. Good.\n- `params` — correctly awaited in `app/chat/[conversationId]/page.tsx:27`. Good.\n- `searchParams` — not consumed anywhere; nothing to await.\n- **`useReducer` mount-time `dispatch({type:'init',...})` in `MessageStream.tsx:87-93`** runs on EVERY mount with `[]` deps — fine, but the `eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` justification (\"re-running on prop change would wipe live state\") only holds because the route remount per `[conversationId]` is what produces fresh state. If you ever switch to `useReducer`'s lazy init via the 3rd-arg initializer, you can drop the effect entirely.\n- **No `'use client'` leak.** `server-session.ts` correctly imports `server-only`. Auth pages and chat components correctly carry `'use client'`. Layouts that need it stay server.\n- **`useTransition` in `LogoutButton.tsx:15` wraps `router.push` but doesn't await the navigation.** React 19 deprecates async `startTransition` semantics on the client router; not strictly wrong but `router.push` doesn't return a promise here.\n- **`useRef<WsClientLike | null>(null)` + mutation during render (`MessageStream.tsx:97-100`)** breaks React 19 + Strict Mode invariants — see bug #2 / #3.\n\n## 4. Cross-LLD risk\n\n- **`MessageDto.errorCode/provider/model` hydration** — the contract makes them `nullable().optional()`. Frontend correctly tolerates missing (line 62-64 of `[conversationId]/page.tsx`: `if (dto.provider) ...`). But `dto.provider === null` is falsy → no copy. Acceptable.\n- **`WsSendFrame.conversationId: z.string().uuid().nullable()`** — frontend sends `liveConvIdRef.current` which can be `null` (line 156-159 of MessageStream). Contract allows it. Backend-api MUST mint on null. Coupling clear.\n- **`MessageListResponse.omittedCount`** — frontend defaults to 0 (`conversations-api.ts:40`). Safe.\n- **`/api/auth/session` endpoint** — `server-session.ts:40` assumes it exists and returns `{userId, email?}`. Backend-api may not expose this exact path; coordinate.\n- **`/api/auth/logout`** — assumed to exist; if missing, `LogoutButton` will show error. Coordinate.\n- **`router.replace(\\`/chat/${conversation_id}\\`)`** is invoked from `start` frame BEFORE the reducer state knows the new conversationId; the navigation immediately triggers unmount/remount of `MessageStream` on the new route. The in-flight stream's `token`/`end` frames may now arrive at the unmounted instance (`onFrame` no-op after close) and the new mount's reducer starts fresh — the user sees the user message vanish mid-stream. Significant UX bug; consider `window.history.replaceState` for URL-only mutation, OR don't unmount on route change for this case.\n\n## 5. Accessibility + design fidelity\n\n- `data-testid` coverage is excellent — every interactive element has one.\n- `aria-label` on every button (Cancel, Send, Retry, Log out, Sign in). Good.\n- `aria-current=\"page\"` on active conversation. Good.\n- `role=\"alert\"` on every error message. Good.\n- `role=\"status\"` + `aria-live=\"polite\"` on omitted indicator + loading. Good.\n- **Missing:** no focus management after `router.replace` (new chat → resume route) — keyboard users get dropped focus.\n- **Missing:** message list is `<ol>` but `aria-label=\"Conversation\"` — keyboard tab order through bubbles is unmanaged.\n- **Design deviation:** prototype `chat.jsx` has provider chips with color (line 49-50 of styles.css defines `--p-openai` etc.); the implementation renders plain text labels. Acceptable for Phase A but flag.\n- **Design deviation:** `OmittedIndicator` uses `⋯` unicode dots; prototype uses an SVG glyph. Minor.\n\n## 6. What was done well\n\n1. **Reducer purity is rigorously enforced** — same-reference return on no-op (`composer-submitted` while locked) is tested as `expect(second).toBe(first)`. Cancel-race terminal-guard via `isTerminal()` is clean and tested.\n2. **`WsClient` correctly isolates from `globalThis.WebSocket.OPEN` static** by capturing `READYSTATE_OPEN = 1` locally so test stubs don't need to mirror class statics. Subtle but right.\n3. **`WsClientLike` exported as a structural subset** of the class for test injection, with the production component lazily constructing the real client behind the same interface. Good separation.\n4. **`auth-fetch` discriminates `AuthError` (401)** vs `ApiError` (other 4xx/5xx with code/message) so route-level callers branch cleanly without re-parsing status. Best-effort JSON-body parse for `code` is appropriately defensive.\n5. **`toReducerMessage` mapper in `[conversationId]/page.tsx`** centralizes the DTO→reducer-Message conversion in one place, and correctly hydrates `canRetry=true` for restored `failed` messages so the Retry button surfaces after reload.\n\n## 7. Quality score\n\n**6**\n\nReducer + WS transport are excellent (8-9 quality). Routing, hydration, and the server↔api URL contract have multiple shipping-blocker bugs (#1, #2, #5, #6, the new-conversation unmount race) that will keep `/chat` from working end-to-end on first run.
